}\\n356: \\n357:     private long sendProducerData(long now) {\\n358:         MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot = metadata.fetchMetadataSnapshot();\\n359:         // get the list of partitions with currentTimeMs);\\n498:             transactionManager.setInFlightCorrelationId(clientRequest.correlationId());\\n499:             client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\\n500: Going \\\" +\\n503:                     \\\"to back off and retry.\\\", targetNode, requestBuilder, e);\\n504:             // We break here so that we pick up the FindCoordinator request immediately.\\n505:             maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\\n506:             return true;\\n507:         }\\n508:     }\\n509: \\n510:     private void maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(TransactionManager.TxnRequestHandler nextRequestHandler) {\\n511:         if (nextRequestHandler.needsCoordinator()) {\\n512:             transactionManager.lookupCoordinator(nextRequestHandler);\\n513:         } else {\\n514:             // For non-coordinator requests, sleep here to prevent a tight loop when no node is available\\n515:             time.sleep(retryBackoffMs);\\n516:             metadata.requestUpdate(false);\\n517:         }\\n518: \\n519:         transactionManager.retry(nextRequestHandler);\\n520:     }\\n521: \\n522:     private void maybeAbortBatches(RuntimeException exception) {\\n523:         if (accumulator.hasIncomplete()) {\\n524:             log.error(\\\"Aborting producer batches due to fatal error\\\", exception);\\n525:             accumulator.abortBatches(exception);\\n526:         }\\n527:     }\\n528: \\n529:     /**\\n530:      * Start closing the sender (won't actually complete until all data is sent out)\\n531:      */\\n532:     public void initiateClose() {\\n533:         // Ensure accumulator is closed first to guarantee that no more appends are accepted after\\n534:         // breaking from the sender loop. Otherwise, we may miss some callbacks when shutting down.\\n535:         this.accumulator.close();\\n536:         this.running = false;\\n537:         this.wakeup();\\n538:     }\\n539: \\n540:     /**\\n541:      * Closes the sender without sending out any pending messages.\\n542:      */\\n543:     public void forceClose() {\\n544:         this.forceClose = true;\\n545:         initiateClose();\\n546:     }\\n547: \\n548:     public boolean isRunning() {\\n549:         return running;\\n550:     }\\n551: \\n552:     private boolean awaitNodeReady(Node node, FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType coordinatorType) throws IOException {\\n553:         if (NetworkClientUtils.awaitReady(client, node, time, requestTimeoutMs)) {\\n554:             if (coordinatorType == FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType.TRANSACTION) {\\n555:                 // Indicate to the transaction manager that the coordinator is ready, allowing it to check ApiVersions\\n556:                 // This allows us to bump transactional epochs even if the coordinator is temporarily unavailable at\\n557:                 // the time when the abortable error is handled\\n558:                 transactionManager.handleCoordinatorReady();\\n559:             }\\n560:             return true;\\n561:         }\\n562:         return false;\\n563:     }\\n564: \\n565:     /**\\n566:      * Handle a produce response\\n567:      */\\n568:     private void handleProduceResponse(ClientResponse response, Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> batches, Map<Uuid, String> topicNames, long now) {\\n569:         RequestHeader requestHeader = response.requestHeader();\\n570:         int correlationId = requestHeader.correlationId();\\n571:         if (response.wasTimedOut()) {\\n572:             log.trace(\\\"Cancelled request with header {} due to the last request to node {} timed out\\\",\\n573:                 requestHeader, response.destination());\\n574:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\\n575:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.REQUEST_TIMED_OUT, String.format(\\\"Disconnected from node %s due to timeout\\\", response.destination())),\\n576:                         correlationId, now, null);\\n577:         } else if (response.wasDisconnected()) {\\n578:             log.trace(\\\"Cancelled request with header {} due to node {} being disconnected\\\",\\n579:                 requestHeader, response.destination());\\n580:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\\n581:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.NETWORK_EXCEPTION, String.format(\\\"Disconnected from node %s\\\", response.destination())),\\n582:                         correlationId, now, null);\\n583:         } else if (response.versionMismatch() != null) {\\n584:             log.warn(\\\"Cancelled request {} due to a version mismatch with node {}\\\",\\n585:                     response, response.destination(), response.versionMismatch());\\n586:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\\n587:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.UNSUPPORTED_VERSION), correlationId, now, null);\\n588:         } else {\\n589:             log.trace(\\\"Received produce response from node {} with correlation id {}\\\", response.destination(), correlationId);\\n590:             // if we have a response, parse it\\n591:             if (response.hasResponse()) {\\n592:                 // Sender should exercise PartitionProduceResponse rather than ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse\\n593:                 // https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/KAFKA-10696\\n594:                 ProduceResponse produceResponse = (ProduceResponse) response.responseBody();\\n595:                 // This will be set by completeBatch.\\n596:                 Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo = new HashMap<>();\\n597:                 produceResponse.data().responses().forEach(r -> r.partitionResponses().forEach(p -> {\\n598:                     ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse partResp = new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(\\n599:                             Errors.forCode(p.errorCode()),\\n600:                             p.baseOffset(),\\n601:                             p.logAppendTimeMs(),\\n602:                             p.logStartOffset(),\\n603:                             p.recordErrors()\\n604:                                 .stream()\\n605:                                 .map(e -> new ProduceResponse.RecordError(e.batchIndex(), e.batchIndexErrorMessage()))\\n606:                                 .collect(Collectors.toList()),\\n607:                             p.errorMessage(),\\n608:                             p.currentLeader());\\n609: \\n610:                     // Version 13 drop topic name and add support to topic id.\\n611:                     // We need to find batch based on topic id and partition index only as\\n612:                     // topic name in the response will be empty.\\n613:                     // For older versions, topic id is zero, and we will find the batch based on the topic name.\\n614:                     TopicPartition tp = (!r.topicId().equals(Uuid.ZERO_UUID) && topicNames.containsKey(r.topicId())) ?\\n615:                             new TopicPartition(topicNames.get(r.topicId()), p.index()) :\\n616:                             new TopicPartition(r.name(), p.index());\\n617: \\n618:                     ProducerBatch batch = batches.get(tp);\\n619:                     if (batch == null) {\\n620:                         throw new IllegalStateException(\\\"Can't find batch created for topic id \\\" + r.topicId() +\\n621:                                 \\\" topic name \\\" + r.name() + \\\" partition \\\" + p.index() + \\\" using \\\" + topicNames);\\n622:                     }\\n623:                     completeBatch(batch, partResp, correlationId, now, partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo);\\n624:                 }));\\n625: \\n626:                 if (!partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.isEmpty()) {\\n627:                     List<Node> leaderNodes = produceResponse.data().nodeEndpoints().stream()\\n628:                         .map(e -> new Node(e.nodeId(), e.host(), e.port(), e.rack()))\\n629:                         .filter(e -> !e.equals(Node.noNode()))\\n630:                         .collect(\\n631:                             Collectors.toList());\\n632:                     Set<TopicPartition> updatedPartitions = metadata.updatePartitionLeadership(partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo, leaderNodes);\\n633:                     if (log.isTraceEnabled()) {\\n634:                         updatedPartitions.forEach(\\n635:                             part -> log.debug(\\\"For {} leader was updated.\\\", part)\\n636:                         );\\n637:                     }\\n638:                 }\\n639: \\n640:                 this.sensors.recordLatency(response.destination(), response.requestLatencyMs());\\n641:             } else {\\n642:                 // this is the acks = 0 case, just complete all requests\\n643:                 for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values()) {\\n644:                     completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.NONE), correlationId, now, null);\\n645:                 }\\n646:             }\\n647:         }\\n648:     }\\n649: \\n650:     /**\\n651:      * Complete or retry the given batch of records.\\n652:      *\\n653:      * @param batch The record batch\\n654:      * @param response The produce response\\n655:      * @param correlationId The correlation id for the request\\n656:      * @param now The current POSIX timestamp in milliseconds\\n657:      * @param partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo This will be populated with partitions that have updated leader info.\\n658:      */\\n659:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long correlationId,\\n660:                                long now, Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo) {\\n661:         Errors error = response.error;\\n662: \\n663:         if (error == Errors.MESSAGE_TOO_LARGE && batch.recordCount > 1 && !batch.isDone() &&\\n664:                 (batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 || batch.isCompressed())) {\\n665:             // If the batch is too large, we split the batch and send the split batches again. We do not decrement\\n666:             // the retry attempts in this case.\\n667:             log.warn(\\n668:                 \\\"Got error produce response in correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, splitting and retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\\\",\\n669:                 correlationId,\\n670:                 batch.topicPartition,\\n671:                 this.retries - batch.attempts(),\\n672:                 formatErrMsg(response));\\n673:             if (transactionManager != null)\\n674:                 transactionManager.removeInFlightBatch(batch);\\n675:             this.accumulator.splitAndReenqueue(batch);\\n676:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\\n677:             this.sensors.recordBatchSplit();\\n678:         } else if (error != Errors.NONE) {\\n679:             if (canRetry(batch, response, now)) {\\n680:                 log.warn(\\n681:                     \\\"Got error produce response with correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\\\",\\n682:                     correlationId,\\n683:                     batch.topicPartition,\\n684:                     this.retries - batch.attempts() - 1,\\n685:                     formatErrMsg(response));\\n686:                 reenqueueBatch(batch, now);\\n687:             } else if (error == Errors.DUPLICATE_SEQUENCE_NUMBER) {\\n688:                 // If we have received a duplicate sequence error, it means that the sequence number has advanced beyond\\n689:                 // the sequence of the current batch, and we haven't retained batch metadata on the broker to return\\n690:                 // the correct offset and timestamp.\\n691:                 //\\n692:                 // The only thing we can do is to return success to the user and not return a valid offset and timestamp.\\n693:                 completeBatch(batch, response);\\n694:             } else {\\n695:                 // tell the user the result of their request. We only adjust sequence numbers if the batch didn't exhaust\\n696:                 // its retries -- if it did, we don't know whether the sequence number was accepted or not, and\\n697:                 // thus it is not safe to reassign the sequence.\\n698:                 failBatch(batch, response, batch.attempts() < this.retries);\\n699:             }\\n700:             if (error.exception() instanceof InvalidMetadataException) {\\n701:                 if (error.exception() instanceof UnknownTopicOrPartitionException) {\\n702:                     log.warn(\\\"Received unknown topic or partition error in produce request on partition {}. The \\\" +\\n703:                             \\\"topic-partition may not exist or the user may not have Describe access to it\\\",\\n704:                         batch.topicPartition);\\n705:                 } else {\\n706:                     log.warn(\\\"Received invalid metadata error in produce request on partition {} due to {} Going \\\" +\\n707:                             \\\"to request metadata update now\\\", batch.topicPartition, error.exception(response.errorMessage).toString());\\n708:                 }\\n709:                 if (error.exception() instanceof NotLeaderOrFollowerException || error.exception() instanceof FencedLeaderEpochException) {\\n710:                     log.debug(\\\"For {}, received error {}, with leaderIdAndEpoch {}\\\", batch.topicPartition, error, response.currentLeader);\\n711:                     if (partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo != null\\n712:                         && (response.currentLeader.leaderId() != -1 && response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch() != -1)) {\\n713:                         partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.put(batch.topicPartition, new Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch(\\n714:                             Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderId()), Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch())));\\n715:                     }\\n716:                 }\\n717:                 metadata.requestUpdate(false);\\n718:             }\\n719:         } else {\\n720:             completeBatch(batch, response);\\n721:         }\\n722: \\n723:         // Unmute the completed partition.\\n724:         if (guaranteeMessageOrder)\\n725:             this.accumulator.unmutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\\n726:     }\\n727: \\n728:     /**\\n729:      * Format the error from a {@link ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse} in a user-friendly string\\n730:      * e.g \\\"NETWORK_EXCEPTION. Error Message: Disconnected from node 0\\\"\\n731:      */\\n732:     private String formatErrMsg(ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\\n733:         String errorMessageSuffix = (response.errorMessage == null || response.errorMessage.isEmpty()) ?\\n734:                 \\\"\\\" : String.format(\\\". Error Message: %s\\\", response.errorMessage);\\n735:         return String.format(\\\"%s%s\\\", response.error, errorMessageSuffix);\\n736:     }\\n737: \\n738:     private void reenqueueBatch(ProducerBatch batch, long currentTimeMs) {\\n739:         this.accumulator.reenqueue(batch, currentTimeMs);\\n740:         maybeRemoveFromInflightBatches(batch);\\n741:         this.sensors.recordRetries(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\\n742:     }\\n743: \\n744:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\\n745:         if (transactionManager != null) {\\n746:             transactionManager.handleCompletedBatch(batch, response);\\n747:         }\\n748: \\n749:         if (batch.complete(response.baseOffset, response.logAppendTime)) {\\n750:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\\n751:         }\\n752:     }\\n753: \\n754:     private void failBatch(ProducerBatch batch,\\n755:                            ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response,\\n756:                            boolean adjustSequenceNumbers) {\\n757:         final RuntimeException topLevelException;\\n758:         if (response.error == Errors.TOPIC_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\\n759:             topLevelException = new TopicAuthorizationException(Collections.singleton(batch.topicPartition.topic()));\\n760:         else if (response.error == Errors.CLUSTER_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\\n761:             topLevelException = new ClusterAuthorizationException(\\\"The producer is not authorized to do idempotent sends\\\");\\n762:         else\\n763:             topLevelException = response.error.exception(response.errorMessage);\\n764: \\n765:         if (response.recordErrors == null || response.recordErrors.isEmpty()) {\\n766:             failBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n767:         } else {\\n768:             Map<Integer, RuntimeException> recordErrorMap = new HashMap<>(response.recordErrors.size());\\n769:             for (ProduceResponse.RecordError recordError : response.recordErrors) {\\n770:                 // The API leaves us with some awkwardness interpreting the errors in the response.\\n771:                 // We cannot differentiate between different error cases (such as INVALID_TIMESTAMP)\\n772:                 // from the single error code at the partition level, so instead we use INVALID_RECORD\\n773:                 // for all failed records and rely on the message to distinguish the cases.\\n774:                 final String errorMessage;\\n775:                 if (recordError.message != null) {\\n776:                     errorMessage = recordError.message;\\n777:                 } else if (response.errorMessage != null) {\\n778:                     errorMessage = response.errorMessage;\\n779:                 } else {\\n780:                     errorMessage = response.error.message();\\n781:                 }\\n782: \\n783:                 // If the batch contained only a single record error, then we can unambiguously\\n784:                 // use the exception type corresponding to the partition-level error code.\\n785:                 if (response.recordErrors.size() == 1) {\\n786:                     recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, response.error.exception(errorMessage));\\n787:                 } else {\\n788:                     recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, new InvalidRecordException(errorMessage));\\n789:                 }\\n790:             }\\n791: \\n792:             Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions = batchIndex -> {\\n793:                 RuntimeException exception = recordErrorMap.get(batchIndex);\\n794:                 if (exception != null) {\\n795:                     return exception;\\n796:                 } else {\\n797:                     // If the response contains record errors, then the records which failed validation\\n798:                     // will be present in the response. To avoid confusion for the remaining records, we\\n799:                     // return a generic exception.\\n800:                     return new KafkaException(\\\"Failed to append record because it was part of a batch \\\" +\\n801:                         \\\"which had one more more invalid records\\\");\\n802:                 }\\n803:             };\\n804: \\n805:             failBatch(batch, topLevelException, recordExceptions, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n806:         }\\n807:     }\\n808: \\n809:     private void failBatch(\\n810:         ProducerBatch batch,\\n811:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\\n812:         boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\\n813:     ) {\\n814:         failBatch(batch, topLevelException, batchIndex -> topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n815:     }\\n816: \\n817:     private void failBatch(\\n818:         ProducerBatch batch,\\n819:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\\n820:         Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions,\\n821:         boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\\n822:     ) {\\n823:         this.sensors.recordErrors(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\\n824: \\n825:         if (batch.completeExceptionally(topLevelException, recordExceptions)) {\\n826:             if (transactionManager != null) {\\n827:                 try {\\n828:                     // This call can throw an exception in the rare case that there's an invalid state transition\\n829:                     // attempted. Catch these so as not to interfere with the rest of the logic.\\n830:                     transactionManager.handleFailedBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n831:                 } catch (Exception e) {\\n832:                     log.debug(\\\"Encountered error when transaction manager was handling a failed batch\\\", e);\\n833:                 }\\n834:             }\\n835:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\\n836:         }\\n837:     }\\n838: \\n839:     /**\\n840:      * We can retry a send if the error is transient and the number of attempts taken is fewer than the maximum allowed.\\n841:      * We can also retry OutOfOrderSequence exceptions for future batches, since if the first batch has failed, the\\n842:      * future batches are certain to fail with an OutOfOrderSequence exception.\\n843:      */\\n844:     private boolean canRetry(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long now) {\\n845:         return !batch.hasReachedDeliveryTimeout(accumulator.getDeliveryTimeoutMs(), now) &&\\n846:             batch.attempts() < this.retries &&\\n847:             !batch.isDone() &&\\n848:             (transactionManager == null ?\\n849:                     response.error.exception() instanceof RetriableException :\\n850:                     transactionManager.canRetry(response, batch));\\n851:     }\\n852: \\n853:     /**\\n854:      * Transfer the record batches into a list of produce requests on a per-node basis\\n855:      */\\n856:     private void sendProduceRequests(Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> collated, long now) {\\n857:         for (Map.Entry<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> entry : collated.entrySet())\\n858:             sendProduceRequest(now, entry.getKey(), acks, requestTimeoutMs, entry.getValue());\\n859:     }\\n860: \\n861:     /**\\n862:      * Create a produce request from the given record batches\\n863:      */\\n864:     private void sendProduceRequest(long now, int destination, short acks, int timeout, List<ProducerBatch> batches) {\\n865:         if (batches.isEmpty())\\n866:             return;\\n867: \\n868:         final Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> recordsByPartition = new HashMap<>(batches.size());\\n869:         Map<String, Uuid> topicIds = topicIdsForBatches(batches);\\n870: \\n871:         ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceDataCollection tpd = new ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceDataCollection();\\n872:         for (ProducerBatch batch : batches) {\\n873:             TopicPartition tp = batch.topicPartition;\\n874:             MemoryRecords records = batch.records();\\n875:             Uuid topicId = topicIds.get(tp.topic());\\n876:             ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceData tpData = tpd.find(tp.topic(), topicId);\\n877: \\n878:             if (tpData == null) {\\n879:                 tpData = new ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceData()\\n880:                         .setTopicId(topicId).setName(tp.topic());\\n881:                 tpd.add(tpData);\\n882:             }\\n883: \\n884:             tpData.partitionData().add(new ProduceRequestData.PartitionProduceData()\\n885:                     .setIndex(tp.partition())\\n886:                     .setRecords(records));\\n887:             recordsByPartition.put(tp, batch);\\n888:         }\\n889: \\n890:         String transactionalId = null;\\n891:         boolean useTransactionV1Version = false;\\n892:         if (transactionManager != null && transactionManager.isTransactional()) {\\n893:             transactionalId = transactionManager.transactionalId();\\n894:             useTransactionV1Version = !transactionManager.isTransactionV2Enabled();\\n895:         }\\n896: \\n897:         ProduceRequest.Builder requestBuilder = ProduceRequest.builder(\\n898:                 new ProduceRequestData()\\n899:                         .setAcks(acks)\\n900:                         .setTimeoutMs(timeout)\\n901:                         .setTransactionalId(transactionalId)\\n902:                         .setTopicData(tpd),\\n903:                 useTransactionV1Version\\n904:         );\\n905:         // Fetch topic names from metadata outside callback as topic ids may change during the callback\\n906:         // for example if topic was recreated.\\n907:         Map<Uuid, String> topicNames = metadata.topicNames();\\n908: \\n909:         RequestCompletionHandler callback = response -> handleProduceResponse(response, recordsByPartition, topicNames, time.milliseconds());\\n910: \\n911:         String nodeId = Integer.toString(destination);\\n912:         ClientRequest clientRequest = client.newClientRequest(nodeId, requestBuilder, now, acks != 0,\\n913:                 requestTimeoutMs, callback);\\n914:         client.send(clientRequest, now);\\n915:         log.trace(\\\"Sent produce request to {}: {}\\\", nodeId, requestBuilder);\\n916:     }\\n917: \\n918:     private Map<String, Uuid> topicIdsForBatches(List<ProducerBatch> batches) {\\n919:         return batches.stream()\\n920:                 .collect(Collectors.toMap(\\n921:                         b -> b.topicPartition.topic(),\\n922:                         b -> metadata.topicIds().getOrDefault(b.topicPartition.topic(), Uuid.ZERO_UUID),\\n923:                         (existing, replacement) -> replacement)\\n924:                 );\\n925:     }\\n926: \\n927:     /**\\n928:      * Wake up the selector associated with this send thread\\n929:      */\\n930:     public void wakeup() {\\n931:         this.client.wakeup();\\n932:     }\\n933: \\n934:     public maybeRegisterTopicMetrics(String topic) {\\n999:             // if one sensor of the metrics has been registered for the topic,\\n1000:             // then all other sensors should have been registered; and vice versa\\n1001:             String topicRecordsCountName = \\\"topic.\\\" + topic + \\\".records-per-batch\\\";\\n1002:             Sensor topicRecordCount =        log.debug(\"Starting Kafka producer I/O thread.\");\n238: \n239:         // main loop, runs until close is called\n240:         while (running) {\n241:             try {\n242: in the transaction manager, accumulator or waiting for acknowledgment,\n252:         // wait until these are completed.\n253:         while (!forceClose && ((this.accumulator.hasUndrained() || this.client.inFlightRequestCount() > 0) || hasPendingTransactionalRequests())) {\n254:             try {\n255:                 runOnce();\n256:             } catch (Exception e) {\n257:                 log.error(\"Uncaught error in kafka producer I/O thread: \", e);\n258:             }\n259:         }\n260: \n261:         // Abort the transaction if any commit or abort didn't go through the transaction manager's queue\n262:         while (!forceClose && transactionManager != null && transactionManager.hasOngoingTransaction()) {\n263:             if (!transactionManager.isCompleting()) {\n264:                 log.info(\"Aborting incomplete transaction due to shutdown\");\n265:                 try {\n266:                     // It is possible for the transaction manager to throw errors when aborting. Catch these\n267:                     // so as not to interfere with the rest of the shutdown logic.\n268:                     transactionManager.beginAbort();\n269:                 } catch (Exception e) {\n270:                     log.error(\"Error in kafka producer I/O thread while aborting transaction when during closing: \", e);\n271:                     // Force close in case the transactionManager is in error states.\n272:                     forceClose = true;\n273:                 }\n274:             }\n275:             try {\n276:                 runOnce();\n277:             } catch (Exception e) {\n278:                 log.error(\"Uncaught error in kafka producer I/O thread: \", e);\n279:             }\n280:         }\n281: \n282:         if (forceClose) {\n283:             // We need to fail all the incomplete transactional requests and batches and wake up the threads waiting on\n284:             // the futures.\n285:             if (transactionManager != null) {\n286:                 log.debug(\"Aborting incomplete transactional requests due to forced shutdown\");\n287:                 transactionManager.close();\n288:             }\n289:             log.debug(\"Aborting incomplete batches due to forced shutdown\");\n290:             this.accumulator.abortIncompleteBatches();\n291:         }\n292:         try {\n293:             this.client.close();\n294:         } catch (Exception e) {\n295:             log.error(\"Failed to close network client\", e);\n296:         }\n297: \n298:         log.debug(\"Shutdown of Kafka producer I/O thread has completed.\");\n299:     }\n300: \n301:     /**\n302:      * Run a single iteration of sending\n303:      *\n304:      */\n305:     void runOnce() {\n306:         if (transactionManager != null) {\n307:             try {\n308:                 transactionManager.maybeResolveSequences();\n309: \n310:                 RuntimeException lastError = transactionManager.lastError();\n311: \n312:                 // do not continue sending if the transaction manager is in a failed state\n313:                 if (transactionManager.hasFatalError()) {\n314:                     if (lastError != null)\n315:                         maybeAbortBatches(lastError);\n316:                     client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n317:                     return;\n318:                 }\n319: \n320:                 if (transactionManager.hasAbortableError() && shouldHandleAuthorizationError(lastError)) {\n321:                     return;\n322:                 }\n323: \n324:                 // Check whether we need a new producerId. If so, we will enqueue an InitProducerId\n325:                 // request which will be sent below\n326:                 transactionManager.bumpIdempotentEpochAndResetIdIfNeeded();\n327: \n328:                 if (maybeSendAndPollTransactionalRequest()) {\n329:                     return;\n330:                 }\n331:             } catch (AuthenticationException e) {\n332:                 // This is already logged as error, but propagated here to perform any clean ups.\n333:                 log.trace(\"Authentication exception while processing transactional request\", e);\n334:                 transactionManager.authenticationFailed(e);\n335:             }\n336:         }\n337: \n338:         long currentTimeMs = time.milliseconds();\n339:         long pollTimeout = sendProducerData(currentTimeMs);\n340:         client.poll(pollTimeout, currentTimeMs);\n341:     }\n342: \n343:     // We handle {@code TransactionalIdAuthorizationException} and {@code ClusterAuthorizationException} by first\n344:     // failing the inflight requests, then transition the state to UNINITIALIZED so that the user doesn't need to\n345:     // instantiate the producer again.\n346:     private boolean shouldHandleAuthorizationError(RuntimeException exception) {\n347:         if (exception instanceof TransactionalIdAuthorizationException ||\n348:                         exception instanceof ClusterAuthorizationException) {\n349:             transactionManager.failPendingRequests(new AuthenticationException(exception));\n350:             maybeAbortBatches(exception);\n351:             transactionManager.transitionToUninitialized(exception);\n352:             return true;\n353:         }\n354:         return false;\n355:     }\n356: \n357:     private long sendProducerData(long now) {\n358:         MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot = metadata.fetchMetadataSnapshot();\n359:         // get the list of partitions with data ready to send\n360:         RecordAccumulator.ReadyCheckResult result = this.accumulator.ready(metadataSnapshot, now);\n361: \n362:         // if there are any partitions whose leaders are not known yet, force metadata update\n363:         if (!result.unknownLeaderTopics.isEmpty()) {\n364:             // The set of topics with unknown leader contains topics with leader election pending as well as\n365:             // topics which may have expired. Add the topic again to metadata to ensure it is included\n366:             // and request metadata update, since there are messages to send to the topic.\n367:             for (String topic : result.unknownLeaderTopics)\n368:                 this.metadata.add(topic, now);\n369: \n370:             log.debug(\"Requesting metadata update due to unknown leader topics from the batched records: {}\",\n371:                 result.unknownLeaderTopics);\n372:             this.metadata.requestUpdate(false);\n373:         }\n374: \n375:         // remove any nodes we aren't ready to send to\n376:         Iterator<Node> iter = result.readyNodes.iterator();\n377:         long notReadyTimeout = Long.MAX_VALUE;\n378:         while (iter.hasNext()) {\n379:             Node node = iter.next();\n380:             if (!this.client.ready(node, now)) {\n381:                 // Update just the readyTimeMs of the latency stats, so that it moves forward\n382:                 // every time the batch is ready (then the difference between readyTimeMs and\n383:                 // drainTimeMs would represent how long data is waiting for the node).\n384:                 this.accumulator.updateNodeLatencyStats(node.id(), now, false);\n385:                 iter.remove();\n386:                 notReadyTimeout = Math.min(notReadyTimeout, this.client.pollDelayMs(node, now));\n387:             } else {\n388:                 // Update both readyTimeMs and drainTimeMs, this would \"reset\" the node\n389:                 // latency.\n390:                 this.accumulator.updateNodeLatencyStats(node.id(), now, true);\n391:             }\n392:         }\n393: \n394:         // create produce requests\n395:         Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> batches = this.accumulator.drain(metadataSnapshot, result.readyNodes, this.maxRequestSize, now);\n396:         addToInflightBatches(batches);\n397:         if (guaranteeMessageOrder) {\n398:             // Mute all the partitions drained\n399:             for (List<ProducerBatch> batchList : batches.values()) {\n400:                 for (ProducerBatch batch : batchList)\n401:                     this.accumulator.mutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\n402:             }\n403:         }\n404: \n405:         accumulator.resetNextBatchExpiryTime();\n406:         List<ProducerBatch> expiredInflightBatches = getExpiredInflightBatches(now);\n407:         List<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches = this.accumulator.expiredBatches(now);\n408:         expiredBatches.addAll(expiredInflightBatches);\n409: \n410:         // Reset the producer id if an expired batch has previously been sent to the broker. Also update the metrics\n411:         // for expired batches. see the documentation of @TransactionState.resetIdempotentProducerId to understand why\n412:         // we need to reset the producer id here.\n413:         if (!expiredBatches.isEmpty())\n414:             log.trace(\"Expired {} batches in accumulator\", expiredBatches.size());\n415:         for (ProducerBatch expiredBatch : expiredBatches) {\n416:             String errorMessage = \"Expiring \" + expiredBatch.recordCount + \" record(s) for \" + expiredBatch.topicPartition\n417:                 + \":\" + (now - expiredBatch.createdMs) + \" ms has passed since batch creation\";\n418:             failBatch(expiredBatch, new TimeoutException(errorMessage), false);\n419:             if (transactionManager != null && expiredBatch.inRetry()) {\n420:                 // This ensures that no new batches are drained until the current in flight batches are fully resolved.\n421:                 transactionManager.markSequenceUnresolved(expiredBatch);\n422:             }\n423:         }\n424:         sensors.updateProduceRequestMetrics(batches);\n425: \n426:         // If we have any nodes that are ready to send + have sendable data, poll with 0 timeout so this can immediately\n427:         // loop and try sending more data. Otherwise, the timeout will be the smaller value between next batch expiry\n428:         // time, and the delay time for checking data availability. Note that the nodes may have data that isn't yet\n429:         // sendable due to lingering, backing off, etc. This specifically does not include nodes with sendable data\n430:         // that aren't ready to send since they would cause busy looping.\n431:         long pollTimeout = Math.min(result.nextReadyCheckDelayMs, notReadyTimeout);\n432:         pollTimeout = Math.min(pollTimeout, this.accumulator.nextExpiryTimeMs() - now);\n433:         pollTimeout = Math.max(pollTimeout, 0);\n434:         if (!result.readyNodes.isEmpty()) {\n435:             log.trace(\"Nodes with data ready to send: {}\", result.readyNodes);\n436:             // if some partitions are already ready to be sent, the select time would be 0;\n437:             // otherwise if some partition already has some data accumulated but not ready yet,\n438:             // the select time will be the time difference between now and its linger expiry time;\n439:             // otherwise the select time will be the time difference between now and the metadata expiry time;\n440:             pollTimeout = 0;\n441:         }\n442:         sendProduceRequests(batches, now);\n443:         return pollTimeout;\n444:     }\n445: \n446:     /**\n447:      * Returns true if a transactional request is sent or polled, or if a FindCoordinator request is enqueued\n448:      */\n449:     private boolean maybeSendAndPollTransactionalRequest() {\n450:         if (transactionManager.hasInFlightRequest()) {\n451:             // as long as there are outstanding transactional requests, we simply wait for them to return\n452:             client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n453:             return true;\n454:         }\n455: \n456:         if (transactionManager.hasAbortableError()) {\n457:             accumulator.abortUndrainedBatches(transactionManager.lastError());\n458:         } else if (transactionManager.isAborting()) {\n459:             accumulator.abortUndrainedBatches(new TransactionAbortedException());\n460:         }\n461: \n462:         TransactionManager.TxnRequestHandler nextRequestHandler = transactionManager.nextRequest(accumulator.hasIncomplete());\n463:         if (nextRequestHandler == null)\n464:             return false;\n465: \n466:         AbstractRequest.Builder<?> requestBuilder = nextRequestHandler.requestBuilder();\n467:         Node targetNode = null;\n468:         try {\n469:             FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType coordinatorType = nextRequestHandler.coordinatorType();\n470:             targetNode = coordinatorType != null ?\n471:                     transactionManager.coordinator(coordinatorType) :\n472:                     client.leastLoadedNode(time.milliseconds()).node();\n473:             if (targetNode != null) {\n474:                 if (!awaitNodeReady(targetNode, coordinatorType)) {\n475:                     log.trace(\"Target node {} not ready within request timeout, will retry when node is ready.\", targetNode);\n476:                     maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\n477:                     return true;\n478:                 }\n479:             } else if (coordinatorType != null) {\n480:                 log.trace(\"Coordinator not known for {}, will retry {} after finding coordinator.\", coordinatorType, requestBuilder.apiKey());\n481:                 maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\n482:                 return true;\n483:             } else {\n484:                 log.trace(\"No nodes available to send requests, will poll and retry when until a node is ready.\");\n485:                 transactionManager.retry(nextRequestHandler);\n486:                 client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n487:                 return true;\n488:             }\n489: \n490:             if (nextRequestHandler.isRetry())\n491:                 time.sleep(nextRequestHandler.retryBackoffMs());\n492: \n493:             long currentTimeMs = time.milliseconds();\n494:             ClientRequest clientRequest = client.newClientRequest(targetNode.idString(), requestBuilder, currentTimeMs,\n495:                 true, requestTimeoutMs, nextRequestHandler);\n496:             log.debug(\"Sending transactional request {} to node {} with correlation ID {}\", requestBuilder, targetNode, clientRequest.correlationId());\n497:             client.send(clientRequest, currentTimeMs);\n498:             transactionManager.setInFlightCorrelationId(clientRequest.correlationId());\n499:             client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n500:             return true;\n501:         } catch (IOException e) {\n502:             log.debug(\"Disconnect from {} while trying to send request {}. Going \" +\n503:                     \"to back off and retry.\", targetNode, requestBuilder, e);\n504:             // We break here so that we pick up the FindCoordinator request immediately.\n505:             maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\n506:             return true;\n507:         }\n508:     }\n509: \n510:     private void maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(TransactionManager.TxnRequestHandler nextRequestHandler) {\n511:         if (nextRequestHandler.needsCoordinator()) {\n512:             transactionManager.lookupCoordinator(nextRequestHandler);\n513:         } else {\n514:             // For non-coordinator requests, sleep here to prevent a tight loop when no node is available\n515:             time.sleep(retryBackoffMs);\n516:             metadata.requestUpdate(false);\n517:         }\n518: \n519:         transactionManager.retry(nextRequestHandler);\n520:     }\n521: \n522:     private void maybeAbortBatches(RuntimeException exception) {\n523:         if (accumulator.hasIncomplete()) {\n524:             log.error(\"Aborting producer batches due to fatal error\", exception);\n525:             accumulator.abortBatches(exception);\n526:         }\n527:     }\n528: \n529:     /**\n530:      * Start closing the sender (won't actually complete until all data is sent out)\n531:      */\n532:     public void initiateClose() {\n533:         // Ensure accumulator is closed first to guarantee that no more appends are accepted after\n534:         // breaking from the sender loop. Otherwise, we may miss some callbacks when shutting down.\n535:         this.accumulator.close();\n536:         this.running = false;\n537:         this.wakeup();\n538:     }\n539: \n540:     /**\n541:      * Closes the sender without sending out any pending messages.\n542:      */\n543:     public void forceClose() {\n544:         this.forceClose = true;\n545:         initiateClose();\n546:     }\n547: \n548:     public boolean isRunning() {\n549:         return running;\n550:     }\n551: \n552:     private boolean awaitNodeReady(Node node, FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType coordinatorType) throws IOException {\n553:         if (NetworkClientUtils.awaitReady(client, node, time, requestTimeoutMs)) {\n554:             if (coordinatorType == FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType.TRANSACTION) {\n555:                 // Indicate to the transaction manager that the coordinator is ready, allowing it to check ApiVersions\n556:                 // This allows us to bump transactional epochs even if the coordinator is temporarily unavailable at\n557:                 // the time when the abortable error is handled\n558:                 transactionManager.handleCoordinatorReady();\n559:             }\n560:             return true;\n561:         }\n562:         return false;\n563:     }\n564: \n565:     /**\n566:      * Handle a produce response\n567:      */\n568:     private void handleProduceResponse(ClientResponse response, Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> batches, Map<Uuid, String> topicNames, long now) {\n569:         RequestHeader requestHeader = response.requestHeader();\n570:         int correlationId = requestHeader.correlationId();\n571:         if (response.wasTimedOut()) {\n572:             log.trace(\"Cancelled request with header {} due to the last request to node {} timed out\",\n573:                 requestHeader, response.destination());\n574:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\n575:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.REQUEST_TIMED_OUT, String.format(\"Disconnected from node %s due to timeout\", response.destination())),\n576:                         correlationId, now, null);\n577:         } else if (response.wasDisconnected()) {\n578:             log.trace(\"Cancelled request with header {} due to node {} being disconnected\",\n579:                 requestHeader, response.destination());\n580:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\n581:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.NETWORK_EXCEPTION, String.format(\"Disconnected from node %s\", response.destination())),\n582:                         correlationId, now, null);\n583:         } else if (response.versionMismatch() != null) {\n584:             log.warn(\"Cancelled request {} due to a version mismatch with node {}\",\n585:                     response, response.destination(), response.versionMismatch());\n586:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\n587:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.UNSUPPORTED_VERSION), correlationId, now, null);\n588:         } else {\n589:             log.trace(\"Received produce response from node {} with correlation id {}\", response.destination(), correlationId);\n590:             // if we have a response, parse it\n591:             if (response.hasResponse()) {\n592:                 // Sender should exercise PartitionProduceResponse rather than ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse\n593:                 // https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/KAFKA-10696\n594:                 ProduceResponse produceResponse = (ProduceResponse) response.responseBody();\n595:                 // This will be set by completeBatch.\n596:                 Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo = new HashMap<>();\n597:                 produceResponse.data().responses().forEach(r -> r.partitionResponses().forEach(p -> {\n598:                     ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse partResp = new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(\n599:                             Errors.forCode(p.errorCode()),\n600:                             p.baseOffset(),\n601:                             p.logAppendTimeMs(),\n602:                             p.logStartOffset(),\n603:                             p.recordErrors()\n604:                                 .stream()\n605:                                 .map(e -> new ProduceResponse.RecordError(e.batchIndex(), e.batchIndexErrorMessage()))\n606:                                 .collect(Collectors.toList()),\n607:                             p.errorMessage(),\n608:                             p.currentLeader());\n609: \n610:                     // Version 13 drop topic name and add support to topic id.\n611:                     // We need to find batch based on topic id and partition index only as\n612:                     // topic name in the response will be empty.\n613:                     // For older versions, topic id is zero, and we will find the batch based on the topic name.\n614:                     TopicPartition tp = (!r.topicId().equals(Uuid.ZERO_UUID) && topicNames.containsKey(r.topicId())) ?\n615:                             new TopicPartition(topicNames.get(r.topicId()), p.index()) :\n616:                             new TopicPartition(r.name(), p.index());\n617: \n618:                     ProducerBatch batch = batches.get(tp);\n619:                     if (batch == null) {\n620:                         throw new IllegalStateException(\"Can't find batch created for topic id \" + r.topicId() +\n621:                                 \" topic name \" + r.name() + \" partition \" + p.index() + \" using \" + topicNames);\n622:                     }\n623:                     completeBatch(batch, partResp, correlationId, now, partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo);\n624:                 }));\n625: \n626:                 if (!partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.isEmpty()) {\n627:                     List<Node> leaderNodes = produceResponse.data().nodeEndpoints().stream()\n628:                         .map(e -> new Node(e.nodeId(), e.host(), e.port(), e.rack()))\n629:                         .filter(e -> !e.equals(Node.noNode()))\n630:                         .collect(\n631:                             Collectors.toList());\n632:                     Set<TopicPartition> updatedPartitions = metadata.updatePartitionLeadership(partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo, leaderNodes);\n633:                     if (log.isTraceEnabled()) {\n634:                         updatedPartitions.forEach(\n635:                             part -> log.debug(\"For {} leader was updated.\", part)\n636:                         );\n637:                     }\n638:                 }\n639: \n640:                 this.sensors.recordLatency(response.destination(), response.requestLatencyMs());\n641:             } else {\n642:                 // this is the acks = 0 case, just complete all requests\n643:                 for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values()) {\n644:                     completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.NONE), correlationId, now, null);\n645:                 }\n646:             }\n647:         }\n648:     }\n649: \n650:     /**\n651:      * Complete or retry the given batch of records.\n652:      *\n653:      * @param batch The record batch\n654:      * @param response The produce response\n655:      * @param correlationId The correlation id for the request\n656:      * @param now The current POSIX timestamp in milliseconds\n657:      * @param partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo This will be populated with partitions that have updated leader info.\n658:      */\n659:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long correlationId,\n660:                                long now, Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo) {\n661:         Errors error = response.error;\n662: \n663:         if (error == Errors.MESSAGE_TOO_LARGE && batch.recordCount > 1 && !batch.isDone() &&\n664:                 (batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 || batch.isCompressed())) {\n665:             // If the batch is too large, we split the batch and send the split batches again. We do not decrement\n666:             // the retry attempts in this case.\n667:             log.warn(\n668:                 \"Got error produce response in correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, splitting and retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\",\n669:                 correlationId,\n670:                 batch.topicPartition,\n671:                 this.retries - batch.attempts(),\n672:                 formatErrMsg(response));\n673:             if (transactionManager != null)\n674:                 transactionManager.removeInFlightBatch(batch);\n675:             this.accumulator.splitAndReenqueue(batch);\n676:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\n677:             this.sensors.recordBatchSplit();\n678:         } else if (error != Errors.NONE) {\n679:             if (canRetry(batch, response, now)) {\n680:                 log.warn(\n681:                     \"Got error produce response with correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\",\n682:                     correlationId,\n683:                     batch.topicPartition,\n684:                     this.retries - batch.attempts() - 1,\n685:                     formatErrMsg(response));\n686:                 reenqueueBatch(batch, now);\n687:             } else if (error == Errors.DUPLICATE_SEQUENCE_NUMBER) {\n688:                 // If we have received a duplicate sequence error, it means that the sequence number has advanced beyond\n689:                 // the sequence of the current batch, and we haven't retained batch metadata on the broker to return\n690:                 // the correct offset and timestamp.\n691:                 //\n692:                 // The only thing we can do is to return success to the user and not return a valid offset and timestamp.\n693:                 completeBatch(batch, response);\n694:             } else {\n695:                 // tell the user the result of their request. We only adjust sequence numbers if the batch didn't exhaust\n696:                 // its retries -- if it did, we don't know whether the sequence number was accepted or not, and\n697:                 // thus it is not safe to reassign the sequence.\n698:                 failBatch(batch, response, batch.attempts() < this.retries);\n699:             }\n700:             if (error.exception() instanceof InvalidMetadataException) {\n701:                 if (error.exception() instanceof UnknownTopicOrPartitionException) {\n702:                     log.warn(\"Received unknown topic or partition error in produce request on partition {}. The \" +\n703:                             \"topic-partition may not exist or the user may not have Describe access to it\",\n704:                         batch.topicPartition);\n705:                 } else {\n706:                     log.warn(\"Received invalid metadata error in produce request on partition {} due to {} Going \" +\n707:                             \"to request metadata update now\", batch.topicPartition, error.exception(response.errorMessage).toString());\n708:                 }\n709:                 if (error.exception() instanceof NotLeaderOrFollowerException || error.exception() instanceof FencedLeaderEpochException) {\n710:                     log.debug(\"For {}, received error {}, with leaderIdAndEpoch {}\", batch.topicPartition, error, response.currentLeader);\n711:                     if (partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo != null\n712:                         && (response.currentLeader.leaderId() != -1 && response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch() != -1)) {\n713:                         partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.put(batch.topicPartition, new Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch(\n714:                             Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderId()), Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch())));\n715:                     }\n716:                 }\n717:                 metadata.requestUpdate(false);\n718:             }\n719:         } else {\n720:             completeBatch(batch, response);\n721:         }\n722: \n723:         // Unmute the completed partition.\n724:         if (guaranteeMessageOrder)\n725:             this.accumulator.unmutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\n726:     }\n727: \n728:     /**\n729:      * Format the error from a {@link ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse} in a user-friendly string\n730:      * e.g \"NETWORK_EXCEPTION. Error Message: Disconnected from node 0\"\n731:      */\n732:     private String formatErrMsg(ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\n733:         String errorMessageSuffix = (response.errorMessage == null || response.errorMessage.isEmpty()) ?\n734:                 \"\" : String.format(\". Error Message: %s\", response.errorMessage);\n735:         return String.format(\"%s%s\", response.error, errorMessageSuffix);\n736:     }\n737: \n738:     private void reenqueueBatch(ProducerBatch batch, long currentTimeMs) {\n739:         this.accumulator.reenqueue(batch, currentTimeMs);\n740:         maybeRemoveFromInflightBatches(batch);\n741:         this.sensors.recordRetries(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\n742:     }\n743: \n744:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\n745:         if (transactionManager != null) {\n746:             transactionManager.handleCompletedBatch(batch, response);\n747:         }\n748: \n749:         if (batch.complete(response.baseOffset, response.logAppendTime)) {\n750:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\n751:         }\n752:     }\n753: \n754:     private void failBatch(ProducerBatch batch,\n755:                            ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response,\n756:                            boolean adjustSequenceNumbers) {\n757:         final RuntimeException topLevelException;\n758:         if (response.error == Errors.TOPIC_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\n759:             topLevelException = new TopicAuthorizationException(Collections.singleton(batch.topicPartition.topic()));\n760:         else if (response.error == Errors.CLUSTER_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\n761:             topLevelException = new ClusterAuthorizationException(\"The producer is not authorized to do idempotent sends\");\n762:         else\n763:             topLevelException = response.error.exception(response.errorMessage);\n764: \n765:         if (response.recordErrors == null || response.recordErrors.isEmpty()) {\n766:             failBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\n767:         } else {\n768:             Map<Integer, RuntimeException> recordErrorMap = new HashMap<>(response.recordErrors.size());\n769:             for (ProduceResponse.RecordError recordError : response.recordErrors) {\n770:                 // The API leaves us with some awkwardness interpreting the errors in the response.\n771:                 // We cannot differentiate between different error cases (such as INVALID_TIMESTAMP)\n772:                 // from the single error code at the partition level, so instead we use INVALID_RECORD\n773:                 // for all failed records and rely on the message to distinguish the cases.\n774:                 final String errorMessage;\n775:                 if (recordError.message != null) {\n776:                     errorMessage = recordError.message;\n777:                 } else if (response.errorMessage != null) {\n778:                     errorMessage = response.errorMessage;\n779:                 } else {\n780:                     errorMessage = response.error.message();\n781:                 }\n782: \n783:                 // If the batch contained only a single record error, then we can unambiguously\n784:                 // use the exception type corresponding to the partition-level error code.\n785:                 if (response.recordErrors.size() == 1) {\n786:                     recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, response.error.exception(errorMessage));\n787:                 } else {\n788:                     recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, new InvalidRecordException(errorMessage));\n789:                 }\n790:             }\n791: \n792:             Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions = batchIndex -> {\n793:                 RuntimeException exception = recordErrorMap.get(batchIndex);\n794:                 if (exception != null) {\n795:                     return exception;\n796:                 } else {\n797:                     // If the response contains record errors, then the records which failed validation\n798:                     // will be present in the response. To avoid confusion for the remaining records, we\n799:                     // return a generic exception.\n800:                     return new KafkaException(\"Failed to append record because it was part of a batch \" +\n801:                         \"which had one more more invalid records\");\n802:                 }\n803:             };\n804: \n805:             failBatch(batch, topLevelException, recordExceptions, adjustSequenceNumbers);\n806:         }\n807:     }\n808: \n809:     private void failBatch(\n810:         ProducerBatch batch,\n811:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\n812:         boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\n813:     ) {\n814:         failBatch(batch, topLevelException, batchIndex -> topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\n815:     }\n816: \n817:     private void failBatch(\n818:         ProducerBatch batch,\n819:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\n820:         Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions,\n821:         boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\n822:     ) {\n823:         this.sensors.recordErrors(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\n824: \n825:         if (batch.completeExceptionally(topLevelException, recordExceptions)) {\n826:             if (transactionManager != null) {\n827:                 try {\n828:                     // This call can throw an exception in the rare case that there's an invalid state transition\n829:                     // attempted. Catch these so as not to interfere with the rest of the logic.\n830:                     transactionManager.handleFailedBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\n831:                 } catch (Exception e) {\n832:                     log.debug(\"Encountered error when transaction manager was handling a failed batch\", e);\n833:                 }\n834:             }\n835:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\n836:         }\n837:     }\n838: \n839:     /**\n840:      * We can retry a send if the error is transient and the number of attempts taken is fewer than the maximum allowed.\n841:      * We can also retry OutOfOrderSequence exceptions for future batches, since if the first batch has failed, the\n842:      * future batches are certain to fail with an OutOfOrderSequence exception.\n843:      */\n844:     private boolean canRetry(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long now) {\n845:         return !batch.hasReachedDeliveryTimeout(accumulator.getDeliveryTimeoutMs(), now) &&\n846:             batch.attempts() < this.retries &&\n847:             !batch.isDone() &&\n848:             (transactionManager == null ?\n849:                     response.error.exception() instanceof RetriableException :\n850:                     transactionManager.canRetry(response, batch));\n851:     }\n852: \n853:     /**\n854:      * Transfer the record batches into a list of produce requests on a per-node basis\n855:      */\n856:     private void sendProduceRequests(Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> collated, long now) {\n857:         for (Map.Entry<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> entry : collated.entrySet())\n858:             sendProduceRequest(now, entry.getKey(), acks, requestTimeoutMs, entry.getValue());\n859:     }\n860: \n861:     /**\n862:      * Create a produce request from the given record batches\n863:      */\n864:     private void sendProduceRequest(long now, int destination, short acks, int timeout, List<ProducerBatch> batches) {\n865:         if (batches.isEmpty())\n866:             return;\n867: \n868:         final Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> recordsByPartition = new HashMap<>(batches.size());\n869:         Map<String, Uuid> topicIds = topicIdsForBatches(batches);\n870: \n871:         ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceDataCollection tpd = new ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceDataCollection();\n872:         for (ProducerBatch batch : batches) {\n873:             TopicPartition tp = batch.topicPartition;\n874:             MemoryRecords records = batch.records();\n875:             Uuid topicId = topicIds.get(tp.topic());\n876:             ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceData tpData = tpd.find(tp.topic(), topicId);\n877: \n878:             if (tpData == null) {\n879:                 tpData = new ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceData()\n880:                         .setTopicId(topicId).setName(tp.topic());\n881:                 tpd.add(tpData);\n882:             }\n883: \n884:             tpData.partitionData().add(new ProduceRequestData.PartitionProduceData()\n885:                     .setIndex(tp.partition())\n886:                     .setRecords(records));\n887:             recordsByPartition.put(tp, batch);\n888:         }\n889: \n890:         String transactionalId = null;\n891:         boolean useTransactionV1Version = false;\n892:         if (transactionManager != null && transactionManager.isTransactional()) {\n893:             transactionalId = transactionManager.transactionalId();\n894:             useTransactionV1Version = !transactionManager.isTransactionV2Enabled();\n895:         }\n896: \n897:         ProduceRequest.Builder requestBuilder = ProduceRequest.builder(\n898:                 new ProduceRequestData()\n899:                         .setAcks(acks)\n900:                         .setTimeoutMs(timeout)\n901:                         .setTransactionalId(transactionalId)\n902:                         .setTopicData(tpd),\n903:                 useTransactionV1Version\n904:         );\n905:         // Fetch topic names from metadata outside callback as topic ids may change during the callback\n906:         // for example if topic was recreated.\n907:         Map<Uuid, String> topicNames = metadata.topicNames();\n908: \n909:         RequestCompletionHandler callback = response -> handleProduceResponse(response, recordsByPartition, topicNames, time.milliseconds());\n910: \n911:         String nodeId = Integer.toString(destination);\n912:         ClientRequest clientRequest = client.newClientRequest(nodeId, requestBuilder, now, acks != 0,\n913:                 requestTimeoutMs, callback);\n914:         client.send(clientRequest, now);\n915:         log.trace(\"Sent produce request to {}: {}\", nodeId, requestBuilder);\n916:     }\n917: \n918:     private Map<String, Uuid> topicIdsForBatches(List<ProducerBatch> batches) {\n919:         return batches.stream()\n920:                 .collect(Collectors.toMap(\n921:                         b -> b.topicPartition.topic(),\n922:                         b -> metadata.topicIds().getOrDefault(b.topicPartition.topic(), Uuid.ZERO_UUID),\n923:                         (existing, replacement) -> replacement)\n924:                 );\n925:     }\n926: \n927:     /**\n928:      * Wake up the selector associated with this send thread\n929:      */\n930:     public void wakeup() {\n931:         this.client.wakeup();\n932:     }\n933: \n934:     public static Sensor throttleTimeSensor(SenderMetricsRegistry metrics) {\n935:         Sensor produceThrottleTimeSensor = metrics.sensor(\"produce-throttle-time\");\n936:         produceThrottleTimeSensor.add(metrics.produceThrottleTimeAvg, new Avg());\n937:         produceThrottleTimeSensor.add(metrics.produceThrottleTimeMax, new Max());\n938:         return produceThrottleTimeSensor;\n939:     }\n940: \n941:     /**\n942:      * A collection of sensors for the sender\n943:      */\n944:     private static class SenderMetrics {\n945:         public final Sensor retrySensor;\n946:         public final Sensor errorSensor;\n947:         public final Sensor queueTimeSensor;\n948:         public final Sensor requestTimeSensor;\n949:         public final Sensor recordsPerRequestSensor;\n950:         public final Sensor batchSizeSensor;\n951:         public final Sensor compressionRateSensor;\n952:         public final Sensor maxRecordSizeSensor;\n953:         public final Sensor batchSplitSensor;\n954:         private final SenderMetricsRegistry metrics;\n955:         private final Time time;\n956: \n957:         public SenderMetrics(SenderMetricsRegistry metrics, Metadata metadata, KafkaClient client, Time time) {\n958:             this.metrics = metrics;\n959:             this.time = time;\n960: \n961:             this.batchSizeSensor = metrics.sensor(\"batch-size\");\n962:             this.batchSizeSensor.add(metrics.batchSizeAvg, new Avg());\n963:             this.batchSizeSensor.add(metrics.batchSizeMax, new Max());\n964: \n965:             this.compressionRateSensor = metrics.sensor(\"compression-rate\");\n966:             this.compressionRateSensor.add(metrics.compressionRateAvg, new Avg());\n967: \n968:             this.queueTimeSensor = So ProducerBatch.buffer() returns recordsBuilder.buffer(). Now let me look at the critical section. The issue is:\n\n1. sendProduceRequest() creates a ProduceRequest with MemoryRecords (which wraps the batch's ByteBuffer)\n2. client.send() queues this request\n3. The actual serialization happens asynchronously in the network layer, creating a window where the buffer can be deallocated and reused before the I/O thread reads from it.\n\nThe race condition unfolds like this: sendProduceRequest() queues a request, then failBatch() deallocates and returns the buffer to the pool, which gets reused for a new batch on a different topic. When the network I/O thread finally serializes the original queued request, it reads from the now-corrupted buffer containing the new batch's data, causing messages to appear on the wrong topic. I found the critical piece! At line 608:```java\nSend send = request.toSend(header);\n```\n\nAnd then at line 617:```java\nselector.send(new NetworkSend(clientRequest.destination(), send));\n```\n\nSo the `Send` object is created at line 608, which serializes the request (including the MemoryRecords buffer), and then it's queued to the selector at line 617.\n\nThe issue is that `request.toSend(header)` creates a Send object that will read from the MemoryRecords buffer when it's actually written to the socket. If the buffer is deallocated before the Send object is fully transmitted, the buffer contents will be corrupted.\n\nNow the KEY QUESTION is: when is the Send object actually read/transmitted?Looking at line 645:```java\nthis.selector.poll(Utils.min(timeout, metadataTimeout, telemetryTimeout, defaultRequestTimeoutMs));\n```\n\nThis is where the actual network I/O happens. The selector polls the network and transmits pending Send objects.\n\nSo the race condition is:\n1. Sender thread in sendProduceRequest(): calls client.send() which calls doSend()\n2. doSend() creates a Send object at line 608 and queues it to the selector at line 617\n3. Sender thread in sendProducerData(): continues and calls failBatch() which deallocates the batch buffer\n4. The buffer is returned to the pool and might be reused\n5. Network poll happens: selector.poll() tries to transmit the Send object\n6. But the buffer it points to has been reused for a different batch!\n\nBUT WAIT, in a typical Kafka producer, the Sender thread is the only thread doing these operations. So how can there be a race condition if it's all in one thread?\n\nThe key is ASYNC NETWORK I/O! The selector operates asynchronously. When client.send() is called, it just queues the Send object. The actual transmission happens later during selector.poll(). \n\nThe real problem is an ordering issue within the same thread: the batch buffer gets deallocated and recycled before selector.poll() finishes transmitting the queued request, so the network I/O reads from a buffer that's now been repurposed for different data.\n\nTo pinpoint this, I need to trace the exact sequence in sendProducerData(). The batches are drained, added to inflight, then expired batches are failed (which deallocates their buffers around line 835), and only after that are produce requests sent. The timing between when failBatch() recycles the buffer and when selector.poll() actually transmits the request is where the race condition {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_019Hk9pGJkg8KnM6tFe63qQy","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"OK so I see:\n- Line 395: batches are drained\n- Line 396: addToInflightBatches(batches)\n- Line 406: getExpiredInflightBatches(now) - gets batches from inFlightBatches that have expired\n- Line 407: accumulator.expiredBatches(now) - gets batches from the accumulator that have expired\n- Line 408: merge them\n- Line 415-423: for each expiredBatch, failBatch is called\n- Line 442: sendProduceRequests(batches, now) sends the batches that were just drained\n\nSo here's the KEY: \n- At line 395-396, batches are just drained from the accumulator and added to inFlightBatches\n- At line 406, we check for expiredInflightBatches from inFlightBatches\n- These expiredInflightBatches could be batches from PREVIOUS calls to sendProducerData that are now timing out\n- OR they could be batches that were just added at line 396 that somehow expire immediately (unlikely, but theoretically possible)\n\nBut more importantly, the batches drained at line 395 haven't been SENT yet (that happens at line 442). So the race condition must be about batches that were sent in a PREVIOUS call to sendProducerData().\n\nActually, looking at getExpiredInflightBatches, it gets batches from inFlightBatches that have \"reached delivery timeout\". These are batches that were previously sent (in a previous call to sendProducerData).\n\nSo the sequence is:\n1. Call 1 to sendProducerData:\n   - Batch A is drained and added to inFlightBatches\n   - Batch A is sent via sendProduceRequests()\n   \n2. Call 2 to sendProducerData:\n   - Batch A is still in inFlightBatches\n   - getExpiredInflightBatches detects Batch A as expired (has reached delivery timeout)\n   - failBatch(Batch A) is called, which deallocates Batch A's buffer\n\nThe critical issue is whether the Send object has finished transmitting before the buffer gets deallocated. If the Send is still queued in the NetworkClient waiting to be fully transmitted, deallocating its buffer creates a use-after-free. I need to find where Send objects are removed from the queue after transmission completes.\n\nThe timing is the problem: sendProduceRequest() queues the Send object, but it hasn't actually been transmitted yet. When failBatch() runs, it deallocates the buffer and returns it to the pool. Later, when poll() executes, the selector attempts to transmit that same Send object, but its buffer now contains data from a different batch. The buffer was recycled before transmission finished.\n\nThe specific bug appears at line 418 in failBatch() — it deallocates the buffer without verifying that the corresponding Send object has completed transmission.\n\nLooking more carefully at the sequence: batches get added to inFlightBatches at line 396, but sendProduceRequests() doesn't execute until line 442. This means batches are marked as in-flight before they're actually sent, creating a window where a timeout can trigger deallocation of a buffer that's still queued for transmission.\n\nIf a batch is deallocated at line 418 due to expiration, it won't be in the `batches` collection that sendProduceRequests iterates over, so the deallocation prevents the send from ever occurring. The batch fails without being transmitted to the broker.\n\nHowever, there's a critical timing issue: a batch can be drained and sent at line 442 in one call to sendProducerData, then in a subsequent call, that same batch times out and gets deallocated at line 418 while its Send object is still queued in the NetworkClient waiting to be transmitted. This creates a race condition where the buffer is freed while the Send object is still pending, and when the selector attempts to transmit it, it reads from deallocated memory.\n\nThe solution isn't straightforward—we can't simply deallocate the buffer if the Send object remains in the NetworkClient's queue. Looking at handleProduceResponse, responses indicate successful transmission, and disconnects at line 577-582 fail batches safely since the Send object won't transmit anyway. But what happens when a batch times out without a disconnect? That's where the vulnerability lies.\n\nI need to trace when SendInFlightRequest objects are actually removed from the queue and understand how network errors clean up pending
